            </div>

            </div>

          <!-- Preview -->
          <div v-if="autoInvForm.billingMonth" class="bg-indigo-50 rounded-xl px-4 py-3 text-xs space-y-1">
            <div class="font-black text-indigo-700 uppercase tracking-wide mb-2">預覽將生成</div>
            <div v-for="u in (autoInvForm.tenantId?myUnits.filter(u=>u['租客ID']===autoInvForm.tenantId):myUnits.filter(u=>u['租客ID']&&parseFloat(u['每月租金'])>0))" :key="u['租客ID']"
                 class="flex items-center justify-between">
              <span class="text-slate-700 font-semibold">{{ u['租客姓名'] }}</span>
              <span class="font-black text-indigo-700">{{ u['貨幣符號']||autoInvForm.currency }}{{ fmtNum(u['每月租金']) }}</span>
            </div>
          </div>
          <button @click="runAutoInvoice" :disabled="modalLoading||!autoInvForm.billingMonth"
                  class="w-full py-3.5 gradient-indigo text-white rounded-2xl font-black text-sm shadow-lg disabled:opacity-50">
            <i v-if="modalLoading" class="fa-solid fa-circle-notch spin mr-2"></i>
            <i v-else class="fa-solid fa-file-invoice mr-1.5"></i>自動生成{{ autoInvForm.docType==='收據'?'收據':'發票' }}
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </transition>

  <!-- SUBMIT REPAIR MODAL (TENANT) -->
  <transition name="modal">
    <div v-if="showTenantRepairModal" class="fixed z-40 inset-0 md:flex md:items-center md:justify-center">
      <div class="absolute bottom-0 inset-x-0 md:static bg-white rounded-t-3xl md:rounded-3xl shadow-2xl w-full md:max-w-md md:mx-4">
        <div class="sticky top-0 bg-white px-5 pt-5 pb-3 border-b border-slate-100 flex items-center justify-between">
          <h3 class="text-base font-black text-slate-800">報修申請</h3>
          <button @click="showTenantRepairModal=false" class="w-8 h-8 bg-slate-100 rounded-full flex items-center justify-center text-slate-500"><i class="fa-solid fa-times text-sm"></i></button>
        </div>
        <div class="px-5 py-4 space-y-4 pb-10">
          <div class="bg-amber-50 rounded-xl p-3 flex items-start gap-2.5">
            <i class="fa-solid fa-circle-info text-amber-500 mt-0.5 flex-shrink-0"></i>
            <p class="text-xs text-amber-800 font-medium leading-relaxed">請詳細描述需要維修的問題（位置、現象），業主收到後會儘快安排處理並回覆您。</p>
          </div>
          <div><label class="form-label">問題描述 <span class="text-red-400">*</span></label><textarea v-model="tRepairDesc" rows="5" placeholder="例：廚房水龍頭漏水，已持續兩天…" class="form-input resize-none"></textarea></div>
          <button @click="submitTenantRepair" :disabled="modalLoading" class="w-full py-3.5 bg-amber-500 text-white rounded-2xl font-black text-sm shadow-lg">
            <i v-if="modalLoading" class="fa-solid fa-circle-notch spin mr-2"></i>提交報修申請
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>
  </transition>

</div>

<script>
const { createApp, ref, computed, reactive, watch } = Vue;
createApp({
  setup() {
    const loading = ref(false), modalLoading = ref(false);
    const currentUser = ref(null), requirePasswordChange = ref(false), tempEmail = ref(''), userTier = ref('Free');
    const loginRole = ref('admin'), loginId = ref(''), loginPw = ref(''), showPw = ref(false), loginLoading = ref(false);
    const newPw1 = ref(''), newPw2 = ref('');
    const showRegister = ref(false);
    const regForm = reactive({ name:'', email:'', password:'', currency:'HK$' });
    const defaultCurrency = ref('HK$');
    const currencyOptions = [
      { symbol:'HK$', name:'港幣',   desc:'Hong Kong Dollar' },
      { symbol:'¥',   name:'人民幣', desc:'Chinese Yuan (CNY)' },
      { symbol:'$',   name:'美元',   desc:'US Dollar (USD)' },
      { symbol:'MOP$',name:'澳門幣', desc:'Macanese Pataca' },
      { symbol:'NT$', name:'台幣',   desc:'New Taiwan Dollar' },
      { symbol:'£',   name:'英鎊',   desc:'British Pound (GBP)' },
    ];
    const adminTab = ref('home'), tenantTab = ref('home');
    const allUnits = ref([]), allRepairs = ref([]), allPayments = ref([]), allExpenses = ref([]);
    const paymentFilter = ref('全部'), repairFilter = ref('全部');
    const showUnitModal = ref(false), showExpenseModal = ref(false);
    const showRepairModal = ref(false), showTenantRepairModal = ref(false);
    const showPartialPayModal = ref(false), partialPayTarget = ref(null);
    const partialPayForm = reactive({ amount: '', date: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] });
    const showInvoiceModal = ref(false), invoiceTarget = ref(null);
    const showBillModal = ref(false);
    const billCategory = ref('bill'), billType = ref('rent'), billInnerTab = ref('bulk');
    const singleBillForm = reactive({ tenantId:'', billingMonth: new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7), amount:'', paidAmount:'', receiptDate: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0], remark:'', currency:'HK$', sendEmail:false });
    const utilityRows = ref([]);
    const showHistoryModal = ref(false), historyTarget = ref(null);
    const showDepositModal = ref(false);
    const depositForm = reactive({ tenantId:'', docType:'帳單', receiptDate:new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0], moveOutDate:new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0], depositDeduction:'', deductionReason:'' });
    // New feature state
    const showRentAdjustModal = ref(false), rentAdjustForm = reactive({ tenantId:'', newRent:'', effectiveDate:'', reason:'', updateNow:true });
    const showMonthlyStmtModal = ref(false), monthlyStmtYM = ref(new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7));
    const showAnnualReportModal = ref(false), reportYear = ref(new Date().getFullYear());
    const financeTab = ref('dashboard'), dashboardMonth = ref(new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7));
    const showMemoModal = ref(false), memoTarget = ref(null), memoText = ref('');
    const showChecklistModal = ref(false), checklistTarget = ref(null), checklistType = ref('入住'), checklistItems = ref([]), newChecklistItem = ref('');
    const showArchivedModal = ref(false), archivedTenants = ref([]);
    const showArchiveConfirmModal = ref(false), archiveTarget = ref(null), archiveForm = reactive({ moveOutDate: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0], depositStatus:'已退還', notes:'', extraDeduction:'' });
    // Prepayment
    const showPrepayModal = ref(false), prepayForm = reactive({ tenantId:'', amount:'', date: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0], remark:'' });
    const usePrepayOffset = ref(false), prepayOffsetAmount = ref('');
    // Management fee
    const showMgmtFeeModal = ref(false), mgmtFeeTab = ref('bulk');
    const mgmtFeeForm = reactive({ billingMonth: new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7), dueDate:'', sendEmail:false, docType:'帳單', currency:'HK$', tenantId:'', amount:'', paidAmount:'', receiptDate: new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0], remark:'' });
    // Stripe / plan
    const showUpgradeModal = ref(false), stripeLoading = ref('');
    const showAutoInvoiceModal = ref(false);
    const autoInvForm = reactive({ docType:'帳單', currency:'HK$', tenantId:'', billingMonth: new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7), invPrefix:'INV', sendEmail:false });
    const editingUnit = ref(null), selRepair = ref(null);
    const unitForm = reactive({}), payForm = reactive({'文件類別':'帳單','貨幣符號':'HK$'}), paySendEmail = ref(false);
    const expForm = reactive({}), repReply = reactive({status:'處理中',reply:''}), tRepairDesc = ref('');
    const toast = reactive({show:false, msg:'', type:'info'});
    let toastTimer = null;

    function showToast(msg, type='info') {
      Object.assign(toast,{show:true,msg,type}); clearTimeout(toastTimer);
      toastTimer = setTimeout(()=>{toast.show=false;},3200);
    }
    function gsRun(method,...args) {
      return new Promise((resolve,reject)=>google.script.run.withSuccessHandler(resolve).withFailureHandler(reject)[method](...args));
    }
    function fmtNum(v) {
      const n=parseFloat(v); return(isNaN(n)||v===''||v==null)?'—':n.toLocaleString('zh-CN',{minimumFractionDigits:0,maximumFractionDigits:2});
    }
    function isExpiringSoon(d) {
      if(!d)return false; const diff=(new Date(d)-new Date())/86400000; return diff>=0&&diff<=60;
    }
    const getRepairBadge     = s=>s==='完成'?'badge-emerald':s==='處理中'?'badge-blue':s==='已安排'?'badge-indigo':'badge-amber';
    const getRepairIconBg    = s=>s==='完成'?'bg-emerald-50':s==='處理中'?'bg-blue-50':s==='已安排'?'bg-indigo-50':'bg-amber-50';
    const getRepairIconColor = s=>s==='完成'?'text-emerald-500':s==='處理中'?'text-blue-500':s==='已安排'?'text-indigo-500':'text-amber-500';
    const getPaymentBadge    = s=>s==='已繳費'?'badge-emerald':s==='未繳費'?'badge-red':s==='部分繳費'?'badge-amber':'badge-slate';

    const myUnits = computed(()=>{ if(!currentUser.value)return[]; return currentUser.value.role==='admin'?allUnits.value.filter(u=>u['業主ID']===currentUser.value.id):allUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客ID']===currentUser.value.id||u['Email']===currentUser.value.id); });
    const myRepairs = computed(()=>{ if(!currentUser.value)return[]; return currentUser.value.role==='admin'?allRepairs.value.filter(r=>r['業主ID']===currentUser.value.id):allRepairs.value; });
    const myPayments = computed(()=>{ if(!currentUser.value)return[]; return currentUser.value.role==='admin'?allPayments.value.filter(p=>p['業主ID']===currentUser.value.id):allPayments.value; });
    const myExpenses = computed(()=>!currentUser.value?[]:allExpenses.value.filter(e=>e['業主ID']===currentUser.value.id));
    const todayStr = computed(()=>{const d=new Date();return`${d.getFullYear()}年${d.getMonth()+1}月${d.getDate()}日`;});
    const activeUnits = computed(()=>myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客姓名']).length);
    const pendingPaymentsCount = computed(()=>myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['繳費狀態']==='未繳費'||p['繳費狀態']==='部分繳費').length);
    const pendingRepairsCount  = computed(()=>myRepairs.value.filter(r=>r['處理狀態']!=='完成').length);
    const tenantPending        = computed(()=>myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['繳費狀態']==='未繳費').length);
    const tenantActiveRepairs  = computed(()=>myRepairs.value.filter(r=>r['處理狀態']!=='完成').length);
    const totalRent = computed(()=>fmtNum(myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客姓名']).reduce((s,u)=>s+(parseFloat(u['每月租金'])||0),0)));
    const thisMonthExpense = computed(()=>{ const ym=new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7); return fmtNum(myExpenses.value.filter(e=>(e['日期']||'').startsWith(ym)).reduce((s,e)=>s+(parseFloat(e['金額'])||0),0)); });
    const expiringContracts = computed(()=>myUnits.value.filter(u=>isExpiringSoon(u['合約終止日'])&&u['租客姓名']));
    const filteredPayments = computed(()=>{
      if(paymentFilter.value==='全部') return myPayments.value;
      if(paymentFilter.value==='管理費') return myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['標題項目']&&p['標題項目'].includes('管理費'));
      return myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['繳費狀態']===paymentFilter.value);
    });
    const filteredRepairs  = computed(()=>{ if(repairFilter.value==='全部')return myRepairs.value; if(repairFilter.value==='待處理')return myRepairs.value.filter(r=>r['處理狀態']!=='完成'); return myRepairs.value.filter(r=>r['處理狀態']===repairFilter.value); });
    const historyPayments = computed(()=>!historyTarget.value?[]:allPayments.value.filter(p=>p['租客ID']===historyTarget.value['租客ID']));
    // Tier-based limits
    const tenantCount = computed(()=>myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客ID']).length);
    const maxTenants  = computed(()=>userTier.value==='Max'?Infinity:userTier.value==='Pro'?5:3);
    const canAddTenant    = computed(()=>tenantCount.value < maxTenants.value);
    const canAutoInvoice  = computed(()=>userTier.value==='Pro'||userTier.value==='Max');
    const canUseRepairs   = computed(()=>userTier.value==='Pro'||userTier.value==='Max');
    const canUseExpenses  = computed(()=>userTier.value==='Max');
    const canUseMonthly   = computed(()=>userTier.value==='Max');
    // Management fee computeds
    const mgmtFeePayments = computed(()=>myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['標題項目']&&p['標題項目'].includes('管理費')&&!['預付款','預付款抵扣'].includes(p['文件類別'])));
    const totalMgmtFee = computed(()=>myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客ID']&&parseFloat(u['管理費'])>0).reduce((s,u)=>s+(parseFloat(u['管理費'])||0),0));
    const thisMonthYM = computed(()=>new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7));
    const pendingMgmtCount = computed(()=>mgmtFeePayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']===thisMonthYM.value&&(p['繳費狀態']==='未繳費'||p['繳費狀態']==='部分繳費')).length);
    const collectedMgmtThisMonth = computed(()=>mgmtFeePayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']===thisMonthYM.value).reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0));
    const mgmtCollectionRate = computed(()=>totalMgmtFee.value>0?Math.round(collectedMgmtThisMonth.value/totalMgmtFee.value*100):0);
    const thisMonthActualReceived = computed(()=>{const mp=myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']===thisMonthYM.value);const ded=mp.filter(p=>p['文件類別']==='預付款抵扣').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);return mp.reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0)-2*ded;});
    const thisMonthRentPayments = computed(()=>myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']===thisMonthYM.value&&(p['標題項目']||'').includes('租金')&&!['預付款','預付款抵扣'].includes(p['文件類別'])));
    const repairFeePayments = computed(()=>myPayments.value.filter(p=>['帳單','收據'].includes(p['文件類別'])&&(p['標題項目']||'').includes('維修')));

    function prepayBalanceForTenant(tenantId) {
      const pays = allPayments.value.filter(p => p['租客ID'] === tenantId);
      const added = pays.filter(p => p['文件類別'] === '預付款').reduce((s,p) => s + (parseFloat(p['已付金額']) || 0), 0);
      const used = pays.filter(p => p['文件類別'] === '預付款抵扣').reduce((s,p) => s + (parseFloat(p['已付金額']) || 0), 0);
      return Math.max(added - used, 0);
    }

    const unitSearch = ref('');
    const unitFilter = ref('全部');
    const filteredUnits = computed(()=>{
      let list = myUnits.value;
      if(unitFilter.value==='出租中') list = list.filter(u=>u['租客姓名']);
      else if(unitFilter.value==='空置中') list = list.filter(u=>!u['租客姓名']);
      else if(unitFilter.value==='即將到期') list = list.filter(u=>isExpiringSoon(u['合約終止日'])&&u['租客姓名']);
      if(unitSearch.value.trim()){
        const q = unitSearch.value.trim().toLowerCase();
        list = list.filter(u=>(u['單位地址']||'').toLowerCase().includes(q)||(u['租客姓名']||'').toLowerCase().includes(q));
      }
      return list;
    });

    const anyModal = computed(()=>showUnitModal.value||showBillModal.value||showExpenseModal.value||showRepairModal.value||showTenantRepairModal.value||showRegister.value||showPartialPayModal.value||showInvoiceModal.value||showHistoryModal.value||showDepositModal.value||showRentAdjustModal.value||showMonthlyStmtModal.value||showAnnualReportModal.value||showMemoModal.value||showChecklistModal.value||showArchivedModal.value||showArchiveConfirmModal.value||showUpgradeModal.value||showAutoInvoiceModal.value||showMgmtFeeModal.value||showPrepayModal.value);

    const currentPageTitle = computed(()=>{
      if(currentUser.value?.role==='admin'){const m={home:'概覽',units:'管理單位',payments:'帳單收據',repairs:'維修申請',expenses:'財務概覽',plan:'訂閱方案',help:'使用教學 & 常見問題'};return m[adminTab.value]||'';}
      const m={home:'我的租約',payments:'我的帳單',repairs:'維修申請'};return m[tenantTab.value]||'';
    });

    const adminTabs = [{id:'home',label:'首頁',icon:'fa-solid fa-house'},{id:'units',label:'單位',icon:'fa-solid fa-building'},{id:'payments',label:'帳單',icon:'fa-solid fa-file-invoice-dollar'},{id:'repairs',label:'維修',icon:'fa-solid fa-wrench'},{id:'expenses',label:'概覽',icon:'fa-solid fa-chart-pie'},{id:'plan',label:'方案',icon:'fa-solid fa-crown'},{id:'help',label:'教學',icon:'fa-solid fa-circle-question'}];
    const tenantTabs = [{id:'home',label:'首頁',icon:'fa-solid fa-house'},{id:'payments',label:'帳單',icon:'fa-solid fa-file-invoice-dollar'},{id:'repairs',label:'報修',icon:'fa-solid fa-wrench'}];

    async function doLogin() {
      if(!loginId.value.trim())return showToast('請輸入帳號','error');
      loginLoading.value=true;
      try{const res=await gsRun('serverLogin',loginRole.value,loginId.value.trim(),loginPw.value);
        if(res.requirePasswordChange){requirePasswordChange.value=true;tempEmail.value=res.tempEmail;}
        else if(res.success){currentUser.value=res.user;userTier.value=res.user.tier||'Free';defaultCurrency.value=res.user.currency||'HK$';mgmtFeeForm.currency=defaultCurrency.value;autoInvForm.currency=defaultCurrency.value;singleBillForm.currency=defaultCurrency.value;await loadData();}
        else showToast(res.message||'帳號或密碼錯誤','error');
      }catch(e){showToast(e.message||'登入失敗','error');}
      loginLoading.value=false;
    }
    async function doForgotPassword(){if(!loginId.value.trim())return showToast('請先填入您的 Email','error');try{const res=await gsRun('serverForgotPassword',loginId.value.trim());if(res.success)showToast('臨時密碼已發送至您的 Email','success');else showToast(res.message||'查無此帳號','error');}catch(e){showToast('發送失敗','error');}}
    async function doChangePw(){if(!newPw1.value||!newPw2.value)return showToast('請填寫新密碼','error');if(newPw1.value.length<6)return showToast('密碼至少需要 6 個字元','error');if(newPw1.value!==newPw2.value)return showToast('兩次密碼不一致','error');modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverChangePassword',tempEmail.value,newPw1.value);if(res.success){showToast('密碼設定成功，請重新登入','success');requirePasswordChange.value=false;newPw1.value='';newPw2.value='';}else showToast(res.message||'設定失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast('設定失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}
    async function doRegister(){if(!regForm.name||!regForm.email||!regForm.password)return showToast('請填寫所有欄位','error');if(regForm.password.length<6)return showToast('密碼至少需要 6 個字元','error');if(!regForm.currency)return showToast('請選擇預設貨幣','error');modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverRegister',regForm.email.trim(),regForm.name.trim(),regForm.password,regForm.currency);if(res.success){showToast('註冊成功！請登入','success');loginId.value=regForm.email;showRegister.value=false;}else showToast(res.message||'註冊失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'註冊失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}
    function doLogout(){currentUser.value=null;loginId.value='';loginPw.value='';allUnits.value=[];allRepairs.value=[];allPayments.value=[];allExpenses.value=[];}
    async function loadData(){loading.value=true;try{const d=await gsRun('serverGetAllData',currentUser.value);allUnits.value=d.units||[];allRepairs.value=d.repairs||[];allPayments.value=d.payments||[];allExpenses.value=d.expenses||[];}catch(e){showToast('載入資料失敗','error');}loading.value=false;}

    function nextTenantId(){const nums=allUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客ID']&&/^T\d+$/.test(u['租客ID'])).map(u=>parseInt(u['租客ID'].slice(1)));return 'T'+String((nums.length>0?Math.max(...nums):0)+1).padStart(3,'0');}
    function openAddUnit(){editingUnit.value=null;Object.keys(unitForm).forEach(k=>delete unitForm[k]);unitForm['業主ID']=currentUser.value.id;unitForm['貨幣符號']=defaultCurrency.value;unitForm['租客ID']=nextTenantId();showUnitModal.value=true;}
    function openEditUnit(u){editingUnit.value=u;Object.keys(unitForm).forEach(k=>delete unitForm[k]);Object.assign(unitForm,{...u});showUnitModal.value=true;}
    async function saveUnit(){if(!unitForm['單位地址'])return showToast('請填寫單位地址','error');if(!editingUnit.value&&unitForm['租客ID']&&!canAddTenant.value)return showToast(`${userTier.value} 方案最多管理 ${maxTenants.value} 個租客`,'error');const wU=parseFloat(unitForm['本期用水量 (度/噸)'])||0,eU=parseFloat(unitForm['本期用電量 (度/噸)'])||0,wP=parseFloat(unitForm['水費單價'])||0,eP=parseFloat(unitForm['電費單價'])||0;unitForm['本期水費總額']=Math.round(wU*wP);unitForm['本期電費總額']=Math.round(eU*eP);modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=editingUnit.value?await gsRun('serverUpdateUnitData',{...unitForm}):await gsRun('serverAddUnit',{...unitForm});if(res.success){showToast(editingUnit.value?'已更新單位資料':'已新增單位','success');showUnitModal.value=false;await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'操作失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'操作失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}

    function openAddPayment(){ openBillModal('bill','rent','single'); }
    async function savePayment(){if(!payForm['租客ID'])return showToast('請選擇租客','error');if(!payForm['標題項目'])return showToast('請填寫標題項目','error');if(!payForm['總金額'])return showToast('請填寫總金額','error');modalLoading.value=true;let status='未繳費';if(payForm['文件類別']==='收據'){const paid=parseFloat(payForm['已付金額'])||0,total=parseFloat(payForm['總金額'])||0;status=paid>=total?'已繳費':paid>0?'部分繳費':'未繳費';}const data={...payForm,'記錄ID':'PAY'+new Date().getTime(),'建立日期':new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-TW'),'繳費狀態':status,'自動生成':'否','需發送Email':paySendEmail.value?'是':'否','關聯單據ID':''};try{const res=await gsRun('serverAddPayment',data);if(res.success){showToast('帳單已建立','success');showBillModal.value=false;await loadData();}}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'建立失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}
    async function markPaid(p){try{await gsRun('serverUpdatePaymentStatus',p.rowIndex,'已繳費');showToast('已標記為已繳費','success');await loadData();}catch(e){showToast('操作失敗','error');}}
    async function delPayment(p){if(!confirm(`確定刪除「${p['標題項目']}」？`))return;try{await gsRun('serverDeletePayment',p.rowIndex);showToast('已刪除','success');await loadData();}catch(e){showToast('刪除失敗','error');}}
    function openPartialPay(p){partialPayTarget.value=p;partialPayForm.amount='';partialPayForm.date=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];usePrepayOffset.value=false;prepayOffsetAmount.value='';showPartialPayModal.value=true;}
    async function savePartialPay(){
      const cashAmt=parseFloat(partialPayForm.amount)||0;
      const offsetAmt=usePrepayOffset.value?(parseFloat(prepayOffsetAmount.value)||0):0;
      const totalPay=cashAmt+offsetAmt;
      if(totalPay<=0)return showToast('請填寫收款金額','error');
      const bal=prepayBalanceForTenant(partialPayTarget.value['租客ID']);
      if(offsetAmt>bal)return showToast(`預付款餘額不足（餘額：${(partialPayTarget.value['貨幣符號']||defaultCurrency.value)}${fmtNum(bal)}）`,'error');
      modalLoading.value=true;
      try{
        const res=await gsRun('serverRecordPartialPayment',partialPayTarget.value.rowIndex,totalPay,partialPayForm.date);
        if(!res.success){showToast(res.message||'記錄失敗','error');modalLoading.value=false;return;}
        if(offsetAmt>0){
          const unit=myUnits.value.find(u=>u['租客ID']===partialPayTarget.value['租客ID']);
          const cur=(unit?.['貨幣符號'])||partialPayTarget.value['貨幣符號']||defaultCurrency.value;
          await gsRun('serverAddPayment',{
            '記錄ID':'DED'+new Date().getTime()+Math.random().toString(36).slice(-4),
            '業主ID':currentUser.value.id,'租客ID':partialPayTarget.value['租客ID'],
            '建立日期':new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-TW'),'款項期間':new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7),
            '文件類別':'預付款抵扣','標題項目':'預付款抵扣 — '+partialPayTarget.value['標題項目'],
            '總金額':offsetAmt,'已付金額':offsetAmt,'收款日期':partialPayForm.date,
            '繳費狀態':'已繳費','關聯單據ID':partialPayTarget.value['記錄ID'],
            '自動生成':'否','需發送Email':'否','貨幣符號':cur
          });
        }
        showToast('已記錄收款','success');showPartialPayModal.value=false;usePrepayOffset.value=false;prepayOffsetAmount.value='';await loadData();
      }catch(e){showToast(e.message||'記錄失敗','error');}
      modalLoading.value=false;
    }

    function openPrepayModal(tenantId){prepayForm.tenantId=tenantId||'';prepayForm.amount='';prepayForm.date=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];prepayForm.remark='';showPrepayModal.value=true;}
    async function savePrepay(){
      if(!prepayForm.tenantId)return showToast('請選擇租客','error');
      if(!prepayForm.amount||parseFloat(prepayForm.amount)<=0)return showToast('請填寫有效金額','error');
      modalLoading.value=true;
      const unit=myUnits.value.find(u=>u['租客ID']===prepayForm.tenantId);
      const cur=unit?.['貨幣符號']||defaultCurrency.value;
      try{
        const res=await gsRun('serverAddPrepayment',currentUser.value.id,prepayForm.tenantId,parseFloat(prepayForm.amount),prepayForm.date,prepayForm.remark,cur);
        if(res.success){showToast('預付款已記錄','success');showPrepayModal.value=false;await loadData();}
        else showToast(res.message||'記錄失敗','error');
      }catch(e){showToast(e.message||'記錄失敗','error');}
      modalLoading.value=false;
    }

    function openAddExpense(){Object.keys(expForm).forEach(k=>delete expForm[k]);expForm['日期']=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];expForm['業主ID']=currentUser.value.id;showExpenseModal.value=true;}
    async function saveExpense(){if(!expForm['支出項目'])return showToast('請填寫支出項目','error');if(!expForm['金額'])return showToast('請填寫金額','error');modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverAddExpense',{...expForm});if(res.success){showToast('支出已記錄','success');showExpenseModal.value=false;await loadData();}}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'記錄失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}

    function openRepairDetail(r){selRepair.value=r;repReply.status=r['處理狀態']||'處理中';repReply.reply=r['業主回覆']||'';showRepairModal.value=true;}
    async function saveRepairReply(){modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverUpdateRepair',selRepair.value['記錄ID'],repReply.status,repReply.reply);if(res.success){showToast('已更新維修狀態','success');showRepairModal.value=false;await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'更新失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast('更新失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}
    async function submitTenantRepair(){if(!tRepairDesc.value.trim())return showToast('請描述維修問題','error');modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverAddRepair',{'租客ID':currentUser.value.id,'申請日期':new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-TW'),'事項描述':tRepairDesc.value.trim(),'處理狀態':'處理中'});if(res.success){showToast('報修申請已送出','success');showTenantRepairModal.value=false;tRepairDesc.value='';await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'送出失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'送出失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}

    // Invoice preview
    function openInvoice(p){
      const unit=myUnits.value.find(u=>u['租客ID']===p['租客ID']);
      invoiceTarget.value={...p,_tenantName:unit?.['租客姓名']||'',_address:unit?.['單位地址']||''};
      showInvoiceModal.value=true;
    }
    function printInvoice(){
      const p=invoiceTarget.value; if(!p)return;
      const cur=p['貨幣符號']||defaultCurrency;
      const paid=parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0;
      const total=parseFloat(p['總金額'])||0;
      const owing=Math.max(total-paid,0);
      const isReceipt=p['文件類別']==='收據';
      const docLabel=p['文件類別']==='收據'?'收　　據':p['文件類別']==='退租收據'?'退 租 收 據':p['文件類別']==='退租帳單'?'退 租 帳 單':'帳　　單';
      const statusColor=p['繳費狀態']==='已繳費'?'#065f46':'#991b1b';
      const statusBg=p['繳費狀態']==='已繳費'?'#d1fae5':p['繳費狀態']==='部分繳費'?'#fef3c7':'#fee2e2';
      const tenantName=p['_tenantName']||p['租客ID'];
      const fmt=v=>{const n=parseFloat(v);return isNaN(n)?'0':n.toLocaleString('zh-CN',{minimumFractionDigits:0,maximumFractionDigits:2});};
      const el=document.getElementById('invoice-print-area');
      el.style.display='block';
      el.innerHTML=`
<div style="font-family:'Microsoft JhengHei','微軟正黑體',sans-serif;max-width:680px;margin:0 auto;background:#fff;border:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden">
  <!-- Header -->
  <div style="background:#1e293b;padding:24px 32px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between">
    <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:14px">
      <div style="width:44px;height:44px;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.15);border-radius:10px;display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;font-size:20px;color:#fff">🏢</div>
      <div>
        <div style="color:#fff;font-size:16px;font-weight:900;letter-spacing:1px">物業管理系統</div>
        <div style="color:#94a3b8;font-size:11px;margin-top:2px">Property Management Pro</div>
      </div>
    </div>
    <span style="background:${statusBg};color:${statusColor};padding:5px 14px;border-radius:20px;font-size:12px;font-weight:700">${p['繳費狀態']||'—'}</span>
  </div>
  <!-- Doc title + number -->
  <div style="padding:24px 32px 20px;border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9;display:flex;align-items:flex-end;justify-content:space-between">
    <div>
      <div style="font-size:26px;font-weight:900;color:#1e293b;letter-spacing:4px">${docLabel}</div>
      <div style="font-size:11px;color:#94a3b8;font-family:monospace;margin-top:4px">${p['發票號碼']?'發票號碼：'+p['發票號碼']+'　':''}單據ID：${p['記錄ID']||'—'}</div>
    </div>
    <div style="text-align:right;font-size:12px;color:#64748b;line-height:1.8">
      <div>開單日期：<strong style="color:#1e293b">${p['建立日期']||'—'}</strong></div>
      ${p['款項期間']?`<div>計費期間：<strong style="color:#1e293b">${p['款項期間']}</strong></div>`:''}
    </div>
  </div>
  <!-- Bill From / Bill To -->
  <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9">
    <div style="padding:16px 32px;border-right:1px solid #f1f5f9">
      <div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:#94a3b8;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;margin-bottom:6px">業主（收款方）</div>
      <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#1e293b">${p['業主ID']||'—'}</div>
    </div>
    <div style="padding:16px 32px">
      <div style="font-size:10px;font-weight:700;color:#94a3b8;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:1px;margin-bottom:6px">租客（繳費方）</div>
      <div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:#1e293b">${tenantName}</div>
      ${p['_tenantName']?`<div style="font-size:11px;color:#64748b;margin-top:2px">ID：${p['租客ID']}</div>`:''}
      ${p['_address']?`<div style="font-size:11px;color:#64748b;margin-top:2px">${p['_address']}</div>`:''}
    </div>
  </div>
  <!-- Line items table -->
  <div style="padding:20px 32px">
    <table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse">
      <thead>
        <tr style="background:#1e293b">
          <th style="padding:10px 16px;text-align:left;color:#fff;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:0.5px;border-radius:6px 0 0 6px">項目描述</th>
          <th style="padding:10px 16px;text-align:center;color:#fff;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:0.5px">計費期間</th>
          <th style="padding:10px 16px;text-align:right;color:#fff;font-size:11px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:0.5px;border-radius:0 6px 6px 0">金額</th>
        </tr>
      </thead>
      <tbody>
        <tr style="border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9">
          <td style="padding:14px 16px;font-size:14px;font-weight:600;color:#1e293b">${p['標題項目']||'—'}</td>
          <td style="padding:14px 16px;text-align:center;font-size:13px;color:#64748b">${p['款項期間']||'—'}</td>
          <td style="padding:14px 16px;text-align:right;font-size:15px;font-weight:900;color:#1e293b;font-family:monospace">${cur}${fmt(total)}</td>
        </tr>
      </tbody>
    </table>
  </div>
  <!-- Totals -->
  <div style="margin:0 32px 24px;border:1px solid #e2e8f0;border-radius:8px;overflow:hidden">
    <div style="padding:10px 16px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;background:#f8fafc;border-bottom:1px solid #e2e8f0;font-size:13px">
      <span style="color:#64748b">應繳總額</span><span style="font-weight:700;font-family:monospace;color:#1e293b">${cur}${fmt(total)}</span>
    </div>
    <div style="padding:10px 16px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;border-bottom:1px solid #e2e8f0;font-size:13px">
      <span style="color:#64748b">已付金額</span><span style="font-weight:700;font-family:monospace;color:${paid>0?'#059669':'#94a3b8'}">${paid>0?cur+fmt(paid):'—'}</span>
    </div>
    ${p['收款日期']?`<div style="padding:10px 16px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;border-bottom:1px solid #e2e8f0;font-size:13px"><span style="color:#64748b">收款日期</span><span style="font-weight:600;color:#1e293b">${p['收款日期']}</span></div>`:''}
    <div style="padding:14px 16px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;background:#1e293b">
      <span style="color:#fff;font-weight:700;font-size:14px">尚欠金額</span>
      <span style="color:#fff;font-weight:900;font-size:18px;font-family:monospace">${cur}${fmt(owing)}</span>
    </div>
  </div>
  <!-- Signature area (receipts only) -->
  ${isReceipt?`
  <div style="margin:0 32px 24px;display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:16px">
    <div style="border-top:2px solid #1e293b;padding-top:6px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:center">業主簽署</div>
    <div style="border-top:2px solid #1e293b;padding-top:6px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:center">租客確認</div>
  </div>`:''}
  <!-- Footer -->
  <div style="background:#f8fafc;border-top:1px solid #f1f5f9;padding:14px 32px;display:flex;justify-content:space-between;align-items:center">
    <div style="font-size:10px;color:#94a3b8">本單據由物業管理系統自動生成，具有法律效力 · 如有疑問請聯絡業主</div>
    <div style="font-size:10px;color:#cbd5e1">列印於 ${new Date().toLocaleString('zh-TW')}</div>
  </div>
</div>`;
      setTimeout(()=>{window.print();el.style.display='none';el.innerHTML='';},100);
    }

    // Bulk rent bills
    async function runBulkBills(){modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverGenerateMonthlyRentBills',currentUser.value.id);if(res.success){showToast(`已生成 ${res.created} 張帳單${res.skipped>0?'，跳過 '+res.skipped+' 張重複':''}`,'success');showBillModal.value=false;await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'生成失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'生成失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}

    // Utility bills
    function openUtilityModal(){
      utilityRows.value=myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客姓名']&&u['租客ID']).map(u=>({
        tenantId:u['租客ID'], tenantName:u['租客姓名'], address:u['單位地址']||'',
        waterUsage:'', electricUsage:'',
        waterRate:parseFloat(u['水費單價'])||0, electricRate:parseFloat(u['電費單價'])||0,
        currency:u['貨幣符號']||defaultCurrency
      }));
      billCategory.value='bill'; billType.value='utility'; showBillModal.value=true;
    }
    async function runUtilityBills(){
      const rows=utilityRows.value.filter(u=>(parseFloat(u.waterUsage)||0)>0||(parseFloat(u.electricUsage)||0)>0);
      if(rows.length===0)return showToast('請至少輸入一個單位的用量','error');
      modalLoading.value=true;
      try{const res=await gsRun('serverGenerateUtilityBills',currentUser.value.id,rows.map(u=>({tenantId:u.tenantId,waterUsage:parseFloat(u.waterUsage)||0,electricUsage:parseFloat(u.electricUsage)||0,waterRate:u.waterRate,electricRate:u.electricRate,currency:u.currency})));
        if(res.success){showToast(`已生成 ${res.count} 張水電帳單`,'success');showBillModal.value=false;await loadData();}
        else showToast(res.message||'生成失敗','error');
      }catch(e){showToast(e.message||'生成失敗','error');}
      modalLoading.value=false;
    }

    // CSV export helpers
    function toCSV(rows,fields){const bom='\uFEFF';const header=fields.join(',');const body=rows.map(r=>fields.map(f=>{const v=r[f]!=null?String(r[f]):'';return v.includes(',')||v.includes('"')||v.includes('\n')?'"'+v.replace(/"/g,'""')+'"':v;}).join(',')).join('\n');return bom+header+'\n'+body;}
    function downloadCSV(csv,filename){const a=document.createElement('a');a.href='data:text/csv;charset=utf-8,'+encodeURIComponent(csv);a.download=filename;a.click();}
    function exportPaymentsCSV(){const fields=['記錄ID','建立日期','租客ID','款項期間','標題項目','文件類別','貨幣符號','總金額','已付金額','繳費狀態','收款日期','自動生成'];downloadCSV(toCSV(filteredPayments.value,fields),'帳單記錄.csv');}
    function exportExpensesCSV(){const fields=['日期','支出項目','類別','金額','備註'];downloadCSV(toCSV(myExpenses.value,fields),'支出記錄.csv');}

    // Deposit receipt & lease termination
    function openDepositModal(){Object.keys(depositForm).forEach(k=>depositForm[k]='');depositForm.moveOutDate=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];showDepositModal.value=true;}
    async function runDepositReceipt(){if(!depositForm.tenantId)return showToast('請選擇租客','error');const docType=billCategory.value==='bill'?'帳單':'收據';modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverGenerateDepositReceipt',currentUser.value.id,depositForm.tenantId,depositForm.receiptDate,docType);if(res.success){showToast((docType==='帳單'?'押金發票':'押金收據')+'已生成','success');showBillModal.value=false;await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'生成失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'生成失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}
    async function runLeaseTermination(){if(!depositForm.tenantId)return showToast('請選擇租客','error');modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverGenerateLeaseTermination',currentUser.value.id,{tenantId:depositForm.tenantId,moveOutDate:depositForm.moveOutDate,depositDeduction:depositForm.depositDeduction,deductionReason:depositForm.deductionReason});if(res.success){const msg=`退租結算單已生成，應退押金：${res.currency}${(res.refund||0).toLocaleString()}`;showToast(msg,'success');showDepositModal.value=false;await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'生成失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'生成失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}

    async function sendOverdueReminders(){try{const res=await gsRun('serverSendOverdueReminders',currentUser.value.id);if(res.success)showToast(res.sent>0?`已發送 ${res.sent} 封催款通知`:'目前沒有逾期未繳費帳單','success');else showToast(res.message||'發送失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'發送失敗','error');}}

    // ── Monthly statements
    function openMonthlyStatementModal(){showMonthlyStmtModal.value=true;}
    async function sendMonthlyStatements(){modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverSendMonthlyStatements',currentUser.value.id,monthlyStmtYM.value);if(res.success){showToast(`已發送 ${res.sent} 封月結單`,'success');showMonthlyStmtModal.value=false;}else showToast(res.message||'發送失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'發送失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}

    // ── Rent adjustment
    function openRentAdjustModal(){Object.keys(rentAdjustForm).forEach(k=>rentAdjustForm[k]='');rentAdjustForm.updateNow=true;rentAdjustForm.effectiveDate=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];showRentAdjustModal.value=true;}
    async function saveRentAdjust(){if(!rentAdjustForm.tenantId||!rentAdjustForm.newRent)return showToast('請填寫必要欄位','error');modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverSendRentAdjustmentNotice',currentUser.value.id,{...rentAdjustForm});if(res.success){showToast(`租金調整通知已發送（${res.oldRent}→${res.newRent}）`,'success');showRentAdjustModal.value=false;await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'操作失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'操作失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}

    // ── Annual report computeds
    function incomeCategory(p){const t=p['標題項目']||'',d=p['文件類別']||'';if(d==='押金'||t.includes('押金'))return '押金';if(t.includes('管理費'))return '管理費';if(t.includes('水費')||t.includes('電費')||t.includes('水電'))return '水電費';if(t.includes('維修'))return '維修費';return '租金';}
    function incomeCategoryLabel(p){return incomeCategory(p);}
    const annualSummary = computed(()=>{
      const y=parseInt(reportYear.value);
      const yPay=myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']&&p['款項期間'].startsWith(y+'-')&&!['預付款抵扣','預付款'].includes(p['文件類別']));
      const rent=yPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='租金').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);
      const deposit=yPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='押金').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);
      const mgmt=yPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='管理費').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);
      const utility=yPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='水電費').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);
      const repairFee=yPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='維修費').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);
      const totalIncome=rent+deposit+mgmt+utility+repairFee;
      const totalExpense=myExpenses.value.filter(e=>(e['日期']||'').startsWith(y)).reduce((s,e)=>s+(parseFloat(e['金額'])||0),0);
      return {rent,deposit,mgmt,utility,repairFee,totalIncome,totalExpense,netProfit:totalIncome-totalExpense};
    });
    const annualMonthlyRows = computed(()=>{
      const y=parseInt(reportYear.value);
      return Array.from({length:12},(_,i)=>{
        const m=String(i+1).padStart(2,'0');
        const ym=y+'-'+m;
        const mPay=myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']===ym&&!['預付款抵扣','預付款'].includes(p['文件類別']));
        const rent=mPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='租金').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['總金額'])||0),0);
        const deposit=mPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='押金').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);
        const mgmt=mPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='管理費').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['總金額'])||0),0);
        const utility=mPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='水電費').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['總金額'])||0),0);
        const repairFee=mPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='維修費').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['總金額'])||0),0);
        const paid=mPay.reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);
        const expense=myExpenses.value.filter(e=>(e['日期']||'').startsWith(ym)).reduce((s,e)=>s+(parseFloat(e['金額'])||0),0);
        return {month:y+'年'+parseInt(m)+'月',rent,deposit,mgmt,utility,repairFee,paid,expense,net:paid-expense};
      });
    });
    const dashboardStats = computed(()=>{
      const ym=dashboardMonth.value;
      const mPay=myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']===ym&&!['預付款抵扣','預付款'].includes(p['文件類別']));
      const rentPay=mPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='租金');
      const rent=rentPay.reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['總金額'])||0),0);
      const rentPaid=rentPay.reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);
      const deposit=mPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='押金').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);
      const mgmt=mPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='管理費').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['總金額'])||0),0);
      const utility=mPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='水電費').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['總金額'])||0),0);
      const repairFee=mPay.filter(p=>incomeCategory(p)==='維修費').reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['總金額'])||0),0);
      const expense=myExpenses.value.filter(e=>(e['日期']||'').startsWith(ym)).reduce((s,e)=>s+(parseFloat(e['金額'])||0),0);
      const totalIncome=rentPaid+deposit+mgmt+utility+repairFee;
      return {rent,rentPaid,deposit,mgmt,utility,repairFee,expense,totalIncome,net:totalIncome-expense};
    });
    const dashboardRecentPays = computed(()=>myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']===dashboardMonth.value&&!['預付款抵扣','預付款'].includes(p['文件類別'])));
    const incomeTrend = computed(()=>{const now=new Date();return Array.from({length:12},(_,i)=>{const d=new Date(now.getFullYear(),now.getMonth()-11+i,1);const ym=d.getFullYear()+'-'+String(d.getMonth()+1).padStart(2,'0');const label=String(d.getMonth()+1)+'月';const paid=myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']===ym&&!['預付款抵扣','預付款'].includes(p['文件類別'])).reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0),0);return {ym,label,paid};});});
    const incomeTrendMax = computed(()=>Math.max(1,...incomeTrend.value.map(b=>b.paid)));
    const tenantScores = computed(()=>myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客ID']).map(u=>{const pays=myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['租客ID']===u['租客ID']&&!['預付款','預付款抵扣'].includes(p['文件類別']));const total=pays.length;const paid=pays.filter(p=>p['繳費狀態']==='已繳費').length;const rate=total>0?Math.round(paid/total*100):0;const grade=rate>=90?'A':rate>=70?'B':rate>=50?'C':'D';return {tenantId:u['租客ID'],name:u['租客姓名']||u['租客ID'],address:u['單位地址'],total,paid,rate,grade};}).filter(s=>s.total>0).sort((a,b)=>b.rate-a.rate));
    const yieldData = computed(()=>myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客ID']&&parseFloat(u['物業估值'])>0).map(u=>{const annualRent=(parseFloat(u['每月租金'])||0)*12;const value=parseFloat(u['物業估值'])||0;const yld=value>0?Math.round(annualRent/value*1000)/10:0;return {address:u['單位地址'],annualRent,value,yield:yld};}).sort((a,b)=>b.yield-a.yield));
    const archiveUnpaidBills = computed(()=>!archiveTarget.value?[]:myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['租客ID']===archiveTarget.value['租客ID']&&p['繳費狀態']!=='已繳費'&&!['預付款','預付款抵扣'].includes(p['文件類別'])));
    const archiveDepositRefund = computed(()=>{if(!archiveTarget.value)return 0;const dep=parseFloat(archiveTarget.value['押金'])||0;const unpaid=archiveUnpaidBills.value.reduce((s,p)=>s+(parseFloat(p['總金額'])||0),0);const extra=parseFloat(archiveForm.extraDeduction)||0;return dep-unpaid-extra;});
    const annualUnitRanking = computed(()=>{
      const y=parseInt(reportYear.value);
      const map={};
      myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']&&p['款項期間'].startsWith(y+'-')).forEach(p=>{
        const u=myUnits.value.find(u=>u['租客ID']===p['租客ID']);
        const addr=(u&&u['單位地址'])||p['租客ID'];
        map[addr]=(map[addr]||0)+(parseFloat(p['已付金額'])||0);
      });
      return Object.entries(map).map(([address,total])=>({address,total})).sort((a,b)=>b.total-a.total).slice(0,5);
    });
    function printAnnualReport(){
      const y=reportYear.value;
      const s=annualSummary.value;
      const rows=annualMonthlyRows.value.filter(r=>r.income>0||r.expense>0);
      const el=document.getElementById('invoice-print-area');
      el.style.display='block';
      el.innerHTML=`<div style="font-family:sans-serif;max-width:750px;margin:0 auto;padding:32px">
        <div style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:24px;border-bottom:2px solid #1e293b;padding-bottom:16px">
          <div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:900;color:#1e293b">物業管理系統</div>
          <div style="font-size:16px;font-weight:700;color:#4f46e5;margin-top:4px">${y} 年度財務報表</div>
        </div>
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr 1fr;gap:16px;margin-bottom:24px">
          <div style="border:1px solid #d1fae5;border-radius:8px;padding:14px;text-align:center;background:#f0fdf4"><div style="font-size:11px;color:#6b7280;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">總收入</div><div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:900;color:#059669;margin-top:4px">${defaultCurrency.value}${s.totalIncome.toLocaleString()}</div></div>
          <div style="border:1px solid #fee2e2;border-radius:8px;padding:14px;text-align:center;background:#fff7f7"><div style="font-size:11px;color:#6b7280;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">總支出</div><div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:900;color:#dc2626;margin-top:4px">${defaultCurrency.value}${s.totalExpense.toLocaleString()}</div></div>
          <div style="border:1px solid #e0e7ff;border-radius:8px;padding:14px;text-align:center;background:#eef2ff"><div style="font-size:11px;color:#6b7280;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase">淨利潤</div><div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:900;color:${s.netProfit>=0?'#4f46e5':'#dc2626'};margin-top:4px">${defaultCurrency.value}${s.netProfit.toLocaleString()}</div></div>
        </div>
        <table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;font-size:13px;margin-bottom:24px">
          <thead><tr style="background:#1e293b;color:#fff"><th style="padding:10px;text-align:left">月份</th><th style="padding:10px;text-align:right">應收</th><th style="padding:10px;text-align:right">實收</th><th style="padding:10px;text-align:right">支出</th><th style="padding:10px;text-align:right">淨收益</th></tr></thead>
          <tbody>${rows.map((r,i)=>`<tr style="background:${i%2?'#f8fafc':'#fff'}"><td style="padding:9px 10px;font-weight:600">${r.month}</td><td style="padding:9px 10px;text-align:right">${r.income>0?defaultCurrency.value+r.income.toLocaleString():'—'}</td><td style="padding:9px 10px;text-align:right;color:#059669">${r.paid>0?defaultCurrency.value+r.paid.toLocaleString():'—'}</td><td style="padding:9px 10px;text-align:right;color:#dc2626">${r.expense>0?defaultCurrency.value+r.expense.toLocaleString():'—'}</td><td style="padding:9px 10px;text-align:right;font-weight:700;color:${r.net>=0?'#4f46e5':'#dc2626'}">${r.income>0||r.expense>0?defaultCurrency.value+r.net.toLocaleString():'—'}</td></tr>`).join('')}</tbody>
        </table>
        <div style="font-size:10px;color:#94a3b8;text-align:center;border-top:1px solid #e2e8f0;padding-top:12px">由物業管理系統自動生成 · 列印於 ${new Date().toLocaleString('zh-TW')}</div>
      </div>`;
      setTimeout(()=>{window.print();el.style.display='none';el.innerHTML='';},100);
    }

    // ── Memo
    function openMemo(u){memoTarget.value=u;memoText.value=u['待辦事項']||'';showMemoModal.value=true;}
    async function saveMemo(){modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverUpdateTenantMemo',memoTarget.value.rowIndex,memoText.value);if(res.success){showToast('備忘已儲存','success');showMemoModal.value=false;await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'儲存失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'儲存失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}

    // ── Checklist
    const DEFAULT_CHECKLIST = {
      '入住':['鑰匙交接','門禁卡/遙控器','水錶讀數已記錄','電錶讀數已記錄','冷氣機正常運作','熱水爐正常運作','廚房設備清點完畢','衛浴設備正常','牆壁/地板狀況良好','傢俬清點完畢','租客已收取單位規則'],
      '退租':['收回全部鑰匙','收回門禁卡/遙控器','水錶讀數已記錄','電錶讀數已記錄','牆壁/地板無重大損壞','廚房清潔合格','衛浴清潔合格','傢俬完好歸還','押金結算完成','合約已正式終止','通知相關服務供應商']
    };
    function openChecklist(u){
      checklistTarget.value=u; checklistType.value='入住'; newChecklistItem.value='';
      gsRun('serverGetChecklist',currentUser.value.id,u['租客ID'],'入住').then(res=>{
        checklistItems.value=(res.items||DEFAULT_CHECKLIST['入住'].map(t=>({text:t,checked:false})));
      }).catch(()=>{ checklistItems.value=DEFAULT_CHECKLIST['入住'].map(t=>({text:t,checked:false})); });
      showChecklistModal.value=true;
    }
    function switchChecklistType(type){
      checklistType.value=type;
      gsRun('serverGetChecklist',currentUser.value.id,checklistTarget.value['租客ID'],type).then(res=>{
        checklistItems.value=(res.items||DEFAULT_CHECKLIST[type].map(t=>({text:t,checked:false})));
      }).catch(()=>{ checklistItems.value=DEFAULT_CHECKLIST[type].map(t=>({text:t,checked:false})); });
    }
    function toggleChecklistItem(idx){checklistItems.value[idx].checked=!checklistItems.value[idx].checked;}
    function addChecklistItem(){if(!newChecklistItem.value.trim())return;checklistItems.value.push({text:newChecklistItem.value.trim(),checked:false});newChecklistItem.value='';}
    async function saveChecklist(){modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverSaveChecklist',currentUser.value.id,checklistTarget.value['租客ID'],checklistType.value,JSON.stringify(checklistItems.value));if(res.success)showToast('清單已儲存','success');else showToast(res.message||'儲存失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'儲存失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}
    function printChecklist(){
      const el=document.getElementById('invoice-print-area');
      const u=checklistTarget.value; const type=checklistType.value;
      const done=checklistItems.value.filter(i=>i.checked).length;
      el.style.display='block';
      el.innerHTML=`<div style="font-family:sans-serif;max-width:600px;margin:0 auto;padding:32px">
        <div style="text-align:center;margin-bottom:20px;border-bottom:2px solid #1e293b;padding-bottom:14px">
          <div style="font-size:18px;font-weight:900;color:#1e293b">物業管理系統 · ${type}清單</div>
          <div style="font-size:12px;color:#64748b;margin-top:4px">${u['租客姓名']} · ${u['單位地址']} · ${new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-TW')}</div>
        </div>
        <div style="margin-bottom:16px">
          ${checklistItems.value.map(i=>`<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:8px 0;border-bottom:1px solid #f1f5f9">
            <div style="width:18px;height:18px;border:2px solid ${i.checked?'#059669':'#cbd5e1'};border-radius:4px;background:${i.checked?'#059669':'#fff'};display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:center;flex-shrink:0">${i.checked?'<span style="color:#fff;font-size:12px;font-weight:900">✓</span>':''}</div>
            <span style="font-size:13px;color:${i.checked?'#94a3b8':'#1e293b'};text-decoration:${i.checked?'line-through':'none'}">${i.text}</span>
          </div>`).join('')}
        </div>
        <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:32px;margin-top:32px;padding-top:16px;border-top:1px solid #e2e8f0">
          <div style="border-top:2px solid #1e293b;padding-top:6px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:center">業主簽署</div>
          <div style="border-top:2px solid #1e293b;padding-top:6px;font-size:11px;color:#64748b;text-align:center">租客確認</div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
      setTimeout(()=>{window.print();el.style.display='none';el.innerHTML='';},100);
    }

    // ── Archived tenants
    async function loadArchivedTenants(){try{const res=await gsRun('serverGetArchivedTenants',currentUser.value.id);archivedTenants.value=res.records||[];}catch(e){archivedTenants.value=[];}}
    function openArchiveModal(u){archiveTarget.value=u;archiveForm.moveOutDate=new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];archiveForm.depositStatus='已退還';archiveForm.notes='';showArchiveConfirmModal.value=true;}
    async function confirmArchiveTenant(){modalLoading.value=true;try{const res=await gsRun('serverArchiveTenant',currentUser.value.id,archiveTarget.value.rowIndex,{...archiveForm});if(res.success){showToast('租客已封存，記錄保留','success');showArchiveConfirmModal.value=false;await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'封存失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'封存失敗','error');}modalLoading.value=false;}

    // ── Management Fee
    function openMgmtFeeModal(){ mgmtFeeTab.value='bulk'; mgmtFeeForm.billingMonth=new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7); mgmtFeeForm.sendEmail=false; mgmtFeeForm.tenantId=''; mgmtFeeForm.amount=''; mgmtFeeForm.currency=defaultCurrency.value||'HK$'; showMgmtFeeModal.value=true; }
    function autoFillMgmtFee(){ const u=myUnits.value.find(u=>u['租客ID']===mgmtFeeForm.tenantId); if(u&&parseFloat(u['管理費'])>0) mgmtFeeForm.amount=u['管理費']; mgmtFeeForm.currency=u?.['貨幣符號']||defaultCurrency.value; }
    function getMgmtFeeStatus(tenantId){ const ym=thisMonthYM.value; const p=mgmtFeePayments.value.find(p=>p['租客ID']===tenantId&&p['款項期間']===ym); return p?p['繳費狀態']:'未繳費'; }
    async function runBulkMgmtFee(){
      if(!mgmtFeeForm.billingMonth) return showToast('請選擇計費月份','error');
      const units=myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客ID']&&parseFloat(u['管理費'])>0);
      if(!units.length) return showToast('沒有設定管理費的單位','error');
      modalLoading.value=true;
      const ym=mgmtFeeForm.billingMonth; const [yr,mo]=ym.split('-');
      const existing=myPayments.value.filter(p=>p['款項期間']===ym&&p['標題項目']&&p['標題項目'].includes('管理費')).map(p=>p['租客ID']);
      let created=0,skipped=0;
      try{
        for(const u of units){
          if(existing.includes(u['租客ID'])){skipped++;continue;}
          const fee=parseFloat(u['管理費']);
          const title=`${yr}年${parseInt(mo)}月管理費帳單`;
          const data={'記錄ID':'MGMT'+Date.now()+Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,5),'業主ID':currentUser.value.id,'租客ID':u['租客ID'],'標題項目':title,'款項期間':ym,'文件類別':'帳單','貨幣符號':u['貨幣符號']||defaultCurrency.value,'總金額':fee,'已付金額':0,'收款日期':'','繳費狀態':'未繳費','自動生成':'是','需發送Email':mgmtFeeForm.sendEmail?'是':'否','發票號碼':'MGMT-'+ym.replace('-','')+'-'+u['租客ID'],'建立日期':new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-TW'),'關聯單據ID':''};
          const res=await gsRun('serverAddPayment',data);
          if(res.success) created++;
        }
        showToast(`已生成 ${created} 張管理費帳單${skipped>0?'，跳過 '+skipped+' 張重複':''}`,'success');
        showMgmtFeeModal.value=false; showBillModal.value=false; await loadData();
      }catch(e){showToast(e.message||'生成失敗','error');}
      modalLoading.value=false;
    }
    async function saveSingleMgmtFee(){
      if(!mgmtFeeForm.tenantId) return showToast('請選擇租客','error');
      if(!mgmtFeeForm.amount) return showToast('請填寫管理費金額','error');
      modalLoading.value=true;
      const ym=mgmtFeeForm.billingMonth||new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7);
      const [yr,mo]=ym.split('-');
      const paid=parseFloat(mgmtFeeForm.paidAmount)||0; const total=parseFloat(mgmtFeeForm.amount)||0;
      const status=mgmtFeeForm.docType==='收據'?(paid>=total?'已繳費':paid>0?'部分繳費':'未繳費'):'未繳費';
      const title=`${yr}年${parseInt(mo)}月管理費${mgmtFeeForm.docType==='收據'?'收據':'帳單'}${mgmtFeeForm.remark?' ('+mgmtFeeForm.remark+')':''}`;
      const data={'記錄ID':'MGMT'+Date.now()+Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,5),'業主ID':currentUser.value.id,'租客ID':mgmtFeeForm.tenantId,'標題項目':title,'款項期間':ym,'文件類別':mgmtFeeForm.docType,'貨幣符號':mgmtFeeForm.currency,'總金額':total,'已付金額':paid,'收款日期':mgmtFeeForm.docType==='收據'?mgmtFeeForm.receiptDate:'','繳費狀態':status,'自動生成':'否','需發送Email':'否','發票號碼':'MGMT-'+ym.replace('-','')+'-'+mgmtFeeForm.tenantId,'建立日期':new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-TW'),'關聯單據ID':''};
      try{const res=await gsRun('serverAddPayment',data);if(res.success){showToast('管理費帳單已建立','success');showMgmtFeeModal.value=false;await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'建立失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'建立失敗','error');}
      modalLoading.value=false;
    }

    // ── Stripe / Plan
    async function startStripeCheckout(tier) {
      stripeLoading.value = tier;
      try {
        const res = await gsRun('serverCreateStripeCheckout', currentUser.value.id, tier);
        if (res.success && res.url) {
          (window.top||window).location.href = res.url;
        } else {
          showToast(res.message||'無法開啟付款頁面，請稍後再試','error');
        }
      } catch(e) {
        showToast(e.message||'付款連線失敗','error');
      }
      stripeLoading.value = '';
    }

    async function verifyStripeSubscription() {
      stripeLoading.value = 'verify';
      try {
        const res = await gsRun('serverVerifyStripeSubscription', currentUser.value.id);
        if (res.success) {
          userTier.value = res.tier;
          currentUser.value = { ...currentUser.value, tier: res.tier };
          showToast('訂閱已同步！您現在是 ' + res.tier + ' 方案', 'success');
          showUpgradeModal.value = false;
        } else {
          showToast(res.message || '驗證失敗', 'error');
        }
      } catch(e) {
        showToast(e.message || '驗證失敗', 'error');
      }
      stripeLoading.value = '';
    }

    // ── Auto-invoice (Pro/Max)
    function openAutoInvoiceModal(){
      autoInvForm.billingMonth = new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7);
      autoInvForm.currency = defaultCurrency.value||'HK$';
      autoInvForm.tenantId = '';
      autoInvForm.sendEmail = false;
      showAutoInvoiceModal.value = true;
    }
    async function runAutoInvoice(){
      if(!autoInvForm.billingMonth) return showToast('請選擇計費月份','error');
      if(!canAutoInvoice.value) return showToast('此功能需要 Pro 或 Max 方案','error');
      if(autoInvForm.sendEmail && userTier.value !== 'Max') return showToast('自動發送 Email 需要 Max 方案','error');
      modalLoading.value = true;
      try {
        const targets = autoInvForm.tenantId
          ? myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客ID']===autoInvForm.tenantId)
          : myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客ID']&&parseFloat(u['每月租金'])>0);
        if(targets.length===0){showToast('沒有可生成的租客','error');modalLoading.value=false;return;}
        let created=0, skipped=0;
        const ym = autoInvForm.billingMonth;
        const exists = myPayments.value.map(p=>p['租客ID']+p['款項期間']+autoInvForm.docType);
        for(const u of targets){
          const key = u['租客ID']+ym+autoInvForm.docType;
          if(exists.includes(key)){skipped++;continue;}
          const rent = parseFloat(u['每月租金'])||0;
          const [yr,mo] = ym.split('-');
          const title = `${yr}年${parseInt(mo)}月租金${autoInvForm.docType==='收據'?'收據':'帳單'}`;
          const invNo = `${autoInvForm.invPrefix||'INV'}-${ym.replace('-','')}-${u['租客ID']}`;
          const status = autoInvForm.docType==='收據'?'已繳費':'未繳費';
          const data = {
            '記錄ID':'PAY'+Date.now()+Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,6),
            '業主ID':currentUser.value.id,'租客ID':u['租客ID'],
            '標題項目':title,'款項期間':ym,'文件類別':autoInvForm.docType,
            '貨幣符號':u['貨幣符號']||autoInvForm.currency,'總金額':rent,
            '已付金額':autoInvForm.docType==='收據'?rent:0,
            '收款日期':autoInvForm.docType==='收據'?new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]:'',
            '繳費狀態':status,'自動生成':'是',
            '需發送Email':autoInvForm.sendEmail?'是':'否',
            '發票號碼':invNo,'建立日期':new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-TW'),
            '關聯單據ID':''
          };
          const res = await gsRun('serverAddPayment', data);
          if(res.success) created++;
        }
        showToast(`已生成 ${created} 張${autoInvForm.docType}${skipped>0?'，跳過 '+skipped+' 張重複':''}`,'success');
        showAutoInvoiceModal.value = false;
        await loadData();
      } catch(e){ showToast(e.message||'生成失敗','error'); }
      modalLoading.value = false;
    }

    // ── Override openAddUnit to check tier limit
    function openAddUnitChecked(){
      if(!canAddTenant.value){
        showToast(`${userTier.value} 方案最多管理 ${maxTenants.value} 個租客，請升級方案`,'error');
        setTimeout(()=>showUpgradeModal.value=true, 800);
        return;
      }
      openAddUnit();
    }

    // Auto-populate utilityRows when switching to utility type
    watch(billType,(type)=>{
      if(type==='utility'){
        utilityRows.value=myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客姓名']&&u['租客ID']).map(u=>({
          tenantId:u['租客ID'],tenantName:u['租客姓名'],address:u['單位地址']||'',
          waterUsage:'',electricUsage:'',
          waterRate:parseFloat(u['水費單價'])||0,electricRate:parseFloat(u['電費單價'])||0,
          currency:u['貨幣符號']||defaultCurrency.value||'HK$'
        }));
      }
    });

    function openBillModal(category='bill',type='rent',inner='bulk'){
      billCategory.value=category; billType.value=type; billInnerTab.value=inner;
      Object.assign(singleBillForm,{tenantId:'',billingMonth:new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7),amount:'',paidAmount:'',receiptDate:new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0],remark:'',currency:defaultCurrency.value||'HK$',sendEmail:false});
      if(type==='utility'){ utilityRows.value=myUnits.value.filter(u=>u['租客姓名']&&u['租客ID']).map(u=>({tenantId:u['租客ID'],tenantName:u['租客姓名'],address:u['單位地址']||'',waterUsage:'',electricUsage:'',waterRate:parseFloat(u['水費單價'])||0,electricRate:parseFloat(u['電費單價'])||0,currency:u['貨幣符號']||defaultCurrency.value||'HK$'})); }
      showBillModal.value=true;
    }
    function autoFillSingleBill(){
      const u=myUnits.value.find(u=>u['租客ID']===singleBillForm.tenantId); if(!u)return;
      singleBillForm.currency=u['貨幣符號']||defaultCurrency.value||'HK$';
      if(!singleBillForm.amount){
        if(billType.value==='rent') singleBillForm.amount=u['每月租金']||'';
        else if(billType.value==='mgmt') singleBillForm.amount=u['管理費']||'';
        else if(billType.value==='deposit') singleBillForm.amount=u['押金']||'';
      }
    }
    async function saveSingleBill(){
      if(!singleBillForm.tenantId) return showToast('請選擇租客','error');
      if(!singleBillForm.amount) return showToast('請填寫金額','error');
      const ym=singleBillForm.billingMonth||new Date().toISOString().slice(0,7);
      const [yr,mo]=ym.split('-');
      const typeLabel={rent:'租金',mgmt:'管理費',repair:'維修費',deposit:'押金',utility:'水電費'}[billType.value]||'';
      const docType=billCategory.value==='receipt'?'收據':'帳單';
      const paid=parseFloat(singleBillForm.paidAmount)||0; const total=parseFloat(singleBillForm.amount)||0;
      const status=docType==='收據'?(paid>=total?'已繳費':paid>0?'部分繳費':'未繳費'):'未繳費';
      const title=`${yr}年${parseInt(mo)}月${typeLabel}${docType}${singleBillForm.remark?' ('+singleBillForm.remark+')':''}`;
      modalLoading.value=true;
      const data={'記錄ID':'PAY'+new Date().getTime()+Math.random().toString(36).slice(-4),'文件類別':docType,'業主ID':currentUser.value.id,'租客ID':singleBillForm.tenantId,'建立日期':new Date().toLocaleDateString('zh-TW'),'款項期間':ym,'標題項目':title,'總金額':total,'已付金額':docType==='收據'?paid:'','收款日期':docType==='收據'?singleBillForm.receiptDate:'','繳費狀態':status,'關聯單據ID':'','自動生成':'否','需發送Email':singleBillForm.sendEmail?'是':'否','貨幣符號':singleBillForm.currency||defaultCurrency.value||'HK$'};
      try{const res=await gsRun('serverAddPayment',data);if(res.success){showToast(`${typeLabel}${docType}已建立`,'success');showBillModal.value=false;await loadData();}else showToast(res.message||'建立失敗','error');}catch(e){showToast(e.message||'建立失敗','error');}
      modalLoading.value=false;
    }

    // Feature 6: auto-fill rent when selecting tenant
    watch(()=>payForm['租客ID'],(tid)=>{
      if(!tid)return;
      const u=myUnits.value.find(u=>u['租客ID']===tid);
      if(!u)return;
      const rent=parseFloat(u['每月租金']);
      if(rent&&!payForm['總金額'])payForm['總金額']=rent;
      if(!payForm['標題項目']){const d=new Date();payForm['標題項目']=`${d.getFullYear()}年${d.getMonth()+1}月租金`;}
      if(!payForm['款項期間']){const d=new Date();payForm['款項期間']=d.toISOString().slice(0,7);}
      if(u['貨幣符號'])payForm['貨幣符號']=u['貨幣符號'];
    });

    function closeAllModals(){showUnitModal.value=false;showBillModal.value=false;showExpenseModal.value=false;showRepairModal.value=false;showTenantRepairModal.value=false;showRegister.value=false;showPartialPayModal.value=false;showInvoiceModal.value=false;showHistoryModal.value=false;showDepositModal.value=false;showRentAdjustModal.value=false;showMonthlyStmtModal.value=false;showAnnualReportModal.value=false;showMemoModal.value=false;showChecklistModal.value=false;showArchivedModal.value=false;showArchiveConfirmModal.value=false;showUpgradeModal.value=false;showAutoInvoiceModal.value=false;showMgmtFeeModal.value=false;showPrepayModal.value=false;}

    return {
      loading,modalLoading,currentUser,requirePasswordChange,tempEmail,userTier,defaultCurrency,currencyOptions,
      loginRole,loginId,loginPw,showPw,loginLoading,newPw1,newPw2,showRegister,regForm,
      adminTab,tenantTab,allUnits,allRepairs,allPayments,allExpenses,paymentFilter,repairFilter,
      showUnitModal,showBillModal,billCategory,billType,billInnerTab,singleBillForm,showExpenseModal,showRepairModal,showTenantRepairModal,
      showPartialPayModal,partialPayTarget,partialPayForm,
      showInvoiceModal,invoiceTarget,
      utilityRows,showHistoryModal,historyTarget,
      showDepositModal,depositForm,
      showRentAdjustModal,rentAdjustForm,showMonthlyStmtModal,monthlyStmtYM,
      showAnnualReportModal,reportYear,annualSummary,annualMonthlyRows,annualUnitRanking,
      financeTab,dashboardMonth,dashboardStats,dashboardRecentPays,incomeCategoryLabel,
      incomeTrend,incomeTrendMax,tenantScores,yieldData,
      archiveUnpaidBills,archiveDepositRefund,
      showMemoModal,memoTarget,memoText,
      showChecklistModal,checklistTarget,checklistType,checklistItems,newChecklistItem,
      showArchivedModal,archivedTenants,showArchiveConfirmModal,archiveTarget,archiveForm,
      showPrepayModal,prepayForm,usePrepayOffset,prepayOffsetAmount,prepayBalanceForTenant,
      editingUnit,selRepair,unitForm,payForm,paySendEmail,expForm,repReply,tRepairDesc,toast,
      adminTabs,tenantTabs,currentPageTitle,
      myUnits,myRepairs,myPayments,myExpenses,todayStr,activeUnits,
      pendingPaymentsCount,pendingRepairsCount,tenantPending,tenantActiveRepairs,
      totalRent,thisMonthExpense,expiringContracts,filteredPayments,filteredRepairs,historyPayments,anyModal,
      doLogin,doForgotPassword,doChangePw,doRegister,doLogout,loadData,
      openAddUnit,openEditUnit,saveUnit,
      openAddPayment,savePayment,markPaid,delPayment,openPartialPay,savePartialPay,
      openAddExpense,saveExpense,
      openRepairDetail,saveRepairReply,submitTenantRepair,
      openInvoice,printInvoice,runBulkBills,openUtilityModal,runUtilityBills,openBillModal,autoFillSingleBill,saveSingleBill,
      sendExpiryReminders,openHistory,exportPaymentsCSV,exportExpensesCSV,
      openDepositModal,runDepositReceipt,runLeaseTermination,
      sendOverdueReminders,openMonthlyStatementModal,sendMonthlyStatements,
      openRentAdjustModal,saveRentAdjust,printAnnualReport,
      openMemo,saveMemo,openChecklist,switchChecklistType,toggleChecklistItem,addChecklistItem,saveChecklist,printChecklist,
      loadArchivedTenants,openArchiveModal,confirmArchiveTenant,
      openPrepayModal,savePrepay,
      closeAllModals,fmtNum,isExpiringSoon,
      getRepairBadge,getRepairIconBg,getRepairIconColor,getPaymentBadge,
      // Management fee
      showMgmtFeeModal,mgmtFeeTab,mgmtFeeForm,openMgmtFeeModal,autoFillMgmtFee,getMgmtFeeStatus,runBulkMgmtFee,saveSingleMgmtFee,
      totalMgmtFee,pendingMgmtCount,collectedMgmtThisMonth,mgmtCollectionRate,thisMonthYM,mgmtFeePayments,thisMonthRentPayments,repairFeePayments,
      unitSearch,unitFilter,filteredUnits,
      // Plan/Stripe
      showUpgradeModal,stripeLoading,startStripeCheckout,verifyStripeSubscription,
      showAutoInvoiceModal,autoInvForm,openAutoInvoiceModal,runAutoInvoice,
      tenantCount,maxTenants,canAddTenant,canAutoInvoice,canUseRepairs,canUseExpenses,canUseMonthly,
      openAddUnitChecked,
    };
  }
}).mount('#app');
</script>
<!-- Print invoice area (hidden on screen, shown only when printing) -->
<div id="invoice-print-area" style="display:none"></div>
</body>
</html>
